posted:Posted June 26, 2023
msg:On the way of self-driving, I passed by Suqian for a night of rest. Because I had a furry child, I made a special trip to stay at the Star International Hotel. I did not expect to be satisfied with it unexpectedly. The transportation of the hotel is very convenient. It takes only ten minutes to get off the expressway and walk along Yingbin Avenue. The hotel is located on the shore of Luoma Lake, within a 10-minute walk to the lake, the air is fresh and the environment is quiet. It is rare that it has been rainy for several days. The room is very dry and not damp at all, and it is very comfortable. The room is spacious, the bedding is clean, and you can relax. There is a gym and a swimming pool. The swimming pool is very clear. It is great to take a swim and take a bath to relieve the fatigue of the journey. The hotel is some distance away from the city, but the restaurant offers a la carte, and the food is very good. One thing to note is that the dishes are very large, and a big belly eater like me can hardly hold it. The breakfast is particularly amazing, not to say how luxurious the food is, but the chef's meticulous and thoughtful craftsmanship, and the pastry made first tastes very good. Furry children show their faces, the hotel is friendly to fur children, we must consciously keep the room clean. Fortunately, Maozi is very well-behaved, and he doesn't make noise, tease, scatter, or go to bed in the room, which is very worry-free.
 Mark it, the hotel that you will stay in when you pass by, it is especially recommended.

msg:Bring the dolls to travel to Suqian, book early
Star International Hotel.
Room facilities: I booked a family room with a lake view. The room is huge, about 90 square meters. It is really quite big for a family. There is a bathtub and the toilets are all smart toilets.
Cost-effectiveness: There is no price increase even during the summer vacation, and the price is the same as the usual weekend price, which is full of cost-effectiveness.
Breakfast: There are a lot of varieties, including Chinese and Western styles.
The bed; sleep comfortably, you can fall asleep on your head, and sleep until dawn.
Hygiene: Cleaned very well, not bad!

View of the room:; The room facing west can see the beautiful view of Luoma Lake.
Location and transportation: Located at the core of the national tourist resort, next to the Luoma Lake Visitor Center, it is a local landmark building, and it is within 10 minutes' drive from the two scenic spots of Luoma Lake and Santai Mountain.
Service: There are free fruits, snacks and milk every day, which is very good.
